The new film of the seals has been made, please review it. We immediately sent someone to invite Councilor Gao to the government. It was the date of the regular meeting, and all the commissioners were present. We asked Councilor Gao why he sealed the Wulin Paper Mill. He said he was afraid of destroying evidence. We asked why he did not notify the government. He said he did not trust the provincial government. We asked Councilor Gao on what basis he told the magistrate of Hangzhou County that the Construction Department was influenced by others and that the provincial government was full of corruption. He hesitated and could not answer. When the magistrate of Hangzhou County was summoned, he stared blankly and said nothing. Article 2 of the Supervisory Yuan's rules for investigation states that investigators may temporarily seal off the relevant case files when necessary. Councilor Gao ignored the facts, arbitrarily slandered the government, violated the rules, and illegally sealed the paper mill. What was his intention? It is said that Councilor Gao embezzled public funds when he worked in a financial institution in Peiping. Now he has taken refuge under the National Government and should repent and atone for his past sins in this solemn place. Instead, he is repeating his old tricks, thinking that the government will be perfunctory. His ignorance is truly incorrigible. In addition to submitting a separate report on the entire case of the auction of the Wulin Paper Mill, we hereby submit a report on Councilor Gao's absurd actions in Hangzhou, requesting that you review it and punish him according to the law to deter others and uphold the foundation of the country. We also request that you send another impartial person to Hangzhou for a thorough investigation. If the investigation confirms that Gao Shuo's allegations are true, I and Construction Department Director Shi Ying are willing to carry thorns and go to Beijing to receive the most severe punishment. Respectfully submitted to Yu, the President of the National Government Supervisory Yuan."

Progress of the Longhai Western Section Construction 58

May Be Open to Wenxiang by Mid-July

May Be Open to Tongguan by November

The construction of the new section of the Longhai Western Section from Lingbao to Tongguan, a distance of 72 kilometers, has been progressing rapidly in recent months. The Lingbao Twelve-Arch Iron Bridge was completed on June 22nd. Construction material trains have now reached Chou Sang. At the same time, the tracks are being laid westward. It is heard that the Engineering Bureau has set a deadline of July 15th to open the line to Wenxiang County, about 28 kilometers from Lingbao. In addition to construction material trains, passenger tickets may also be sold. As for west of Wenxiang, because there are still many bridge arches that will take time to construct, it will be necessary to wait until early November to open the line to Tongguan.

The Central Government has long stipulated that the construction cost of the Tongguan to Xi'an section should be funded by the Russo-Geng indemnity. However, it is heard that the issuance of public bonds has not yet been carried out, so the funds have not yet been secured. In order to start construction urgently, the Ministry of Railways is advancing several tens of thousands of yuan per month. The Engineering Bureau has already contracted out the earthwork for the 24-kilometer section from Tongguan to Huayin. The remaining work can only be started when funds are secured. The survey team for the route re-survey is continuing to work west of Huayin and has reached Weinan. It is expected that Xi'an will be reached by mid-August. Tongguan City is located north of the Yellow River and south of high mountains, with a very dangerous terrain. It is heard that the original route was determined to run along the north bank of the Yellow River. However, due to the turbulent waters of the Yellow River and the strong bamboo brushes, the water flow is already approaching the city walls. It is no longer possible to build a road outside the city. The route has now been changed to dig a tunnel outside Jingmen City, passing through the city and emerging from the city on flat ground to reach the West Gate Railway Station. However, since this line passes through the city, more than 100 houses will have to be demolished. The families whose houses are being demolished have jointly requested a change of route. After repeated studies by the Engineering Bureau, it was considered that the demolition of houses along this line was already the minimum possible and could not be avoided in fact. Chairman Yang Hucheng also went to Tongguan to earnestly persuade the families to be demolished, and they have fully complied with the order to demolish their houses. The Tongguan tunnel through the city is 1,070 meters long and will take nine months to complete. Therefore, the Engineering Bureau has first built a temporary station outside the East Gate to facilitate passengers and merchants, so that when the tracks are laid to this point, tickets can be sold and the line can be opened. The tunnel construction does not interfere with this.

Company Law and Implementation Law (Continued) 59

Chapter 3: Application Procedures (Article 22) The registration of the establishment, dissolution, and changes due to mergers of unlimited liability companies shall be applied for by all shareholders. All other registrations shall be applied for by the shareholder representing the company. (Article 23) An unlimited liability company applying for registration due to establishment shall include the company's articles of association, a business budget, and, if any shareholder is a minor, a certificate of consent from the legal guardian. An unlimited liability company applying for registration due to establishment through a merger shall include the notice and announcement stipulated in Article 48, Paragraph 2 of the Company Law, or a certificate of proof that the debt has been paid off or that security has been provided in accordance with Article 49 of the Company Law. (Article 24) An unlimited liability company applying for registration due to dissolution shall state the reason for the dissolution. If the application is made by the heirs, supporting documents shall be attached. If the dissolution is due to a merger, the provisions of Paragraph 3 of the preceding article shall apply mutatis mutandis. (Article 25) An unlimited liability company applying for registration of a change shall state the matters to be changed. If the change is due to a merger, the provisions of Paragraph 3 of Article 23 shall also apply mutatis mutandis. (Article 26) If any matter to be registered by an unlimited liability company requires the consent of all or certain shareholders, a certificate of consent shall be attached. (Article 27) The provisions of Articles 22 to 26 of these rules shall apply mutatis mutandis to limited partnerships. However, in an unlimited liability company, the application shall be made by all shareholders, and the registration in a limited partnership shall be made by all general partners. (Article 28) The registration of the establishment, dissolution, capital increase, capital reduction, issuance of bonds, and changes due to mergers of limited companies shall be applied for by all directors and supervisors. Other registration matters shall be applied for by the director representing the company. (Article 29) A limited company applying for registration due to establishment shall include the following documents: A. If the promoters subscribe for all the shares: 1. The company's articles of association; 2. A list of shareholders; 3. A list of elected directors and supervisors; 4. A certificate of inspection by the competent authority stipulated in Article 91 of the Company Law, and its judgment if reduced; 5. A business budget; 6. A certificate of approval for the record as stipulated in Article 23 of the Company Law Implementation Law. B. If the promoters do not subscribe for all the shares but recruit the required amount separately: 1. The company's articles of association; 2. A list of shareholders; 3. The investigation report and attached documents of the directors, supervisors, or inspectors stipulated in Article 103 of the Company Law; 4. The minutes of the founding meeting; 5. A business budget; 6. A certificate of approval for the record as stipulated in Article 23 of the Company Law Implementation Law. Companies that have started raising capital before the implementation of the Company Law may be exempt from submitting a certificate of approval for the record as stipulated in Article 23 of the Company Law Implementation Law. If applying for registration due to establishment through a merger, the documents stipulated in item 3 of Article 23 shall also be included. (Article 30) A limited company applying for registration due to dissolution shall state the reason for the dissolution. If the dissolution is due to a resolution of the shareholders' meeting, the minutes of the shareholders' meeting regarding the dissolution shall be included. If the dissolution is due to a merger, the provisions of Paragraph 3 of Article 23 shall also apply mutatis mutandis. (Article 31) A limited company applying for registration due to an increase in capital shall include the following documents: 1. The amended articles of association; 2. The minutes of the shareholders' meeting regarding the increase in capital. (Article 32) A limited company applying for registration due to a reduction in capital shall include the following documents: 1. The amended articles of association; 2. The minutes of the shareholders' meeting regarding the reduction in capital; 3. A list of shareholders after the reduction in capital; 4. The documents stipulated in Paragraph 3 of Article 23 of these rules. (Article 33) A limited company applying for registration due to the issuance of company bonds shall include the following documents: 1. The minutes of the shareholders' meeting regarding the issuance of company bonds; 2. The most recent balance sheet; 3. Proof that the issuance of company bonds has been legally announced; 4. Proof that the bond money has been paid in full; 5. A copy of the company bond stub book. (Article 34) A limited company applying for registration due to the repayment or distribution of company bonds shall include proof of the amount repaid. (Article 35) A limited company applying for registration due to the re-election of directors and supervisors shall include a list of the elected directors and supervisors. (Article 36) A limited company applying for registration due to changes in other registration matters shall include the minutes of the shareholders' meeting regarding the resolution to change. (Article 37) A limited company applying for registration due to changes resulting from a merger shall include the documents stipulated in item 1 of Article 23. (Article 38) The registration of the establishment, dissolution, capital increase, capital reduction, and changes due to mergers of limited partnerships shall be applied for by all general partners and all supervisors. The registration of other matters shall be applied for by the general partner representing the company. (Article 39) The registration of the establishment of a limited partnership shall apply mutatis mutandis to the provisions of Paragraph 1 of Article 23 and Paragraphs 1 and 2 of Article 29. (Article 40) The provisions of Articles 31 to 37 shall apply mutatis mutandis to limited partnerships. (Article 41) The registration of the change of a limited partnership to the establishment of a limited company shall be applied for by all directors and supervisors of the established limited company. The application in the preceding paragraph shall state the reason for the change and include the company's articles of association and the minutes of the shareholders' meeting regarding the change of organization. (Article 42) The registration of the establishment, dissolution, and changes of a company's branch shall be applied for by the shareholder representing the company in an unlimited liability company, a limited partnership, or a limited partnership with shares. In a limited company, the application shall be made by the director representing the company. If the company's head office is not located within the Republic of China, the application shall be made by the manager of the first branch. If the manager mentioned in the preceding paragraph is not a citizen of the Republic of China, a certificate of nationality shall be issued by the consul of that country in the locality. (Article 43) When a company whose head office is not located within the Republic of China establishes its first branch within the Republic of China, the matters listed in the application shall be certified by the consul of that country in the locality, and the company's articles of association shall be attached. However, this shall not apply to the establishment of a second branch.

Chapter 4: Supplementary Provisions (Article 44) After the Ministry of Industry and Commerce issues a license, it shall be published in the government gazette. (Article 45) Those who have already applied for registration before the implementation of these rules shall still be handled in accordance with the Provisional Rules for Company Registration. (Article 46) These rules shall come into effect on the same day as the Company Law. (End)

Local Correspondence

Nantong 60

Reorganization of the County Defense Corps Underway Nantong suffered banditry last year. The temporary recruitment and organization of defense corps in each district has been resolved by the County Defense Committee. The recruited members will be dismissed and replaced by a formally drafted defense corps, to be completed by July.

Reorganization of the Finance Bureau After Wang Sheng, the Director of the Nantong County Finance Bureau, took office, the bureau was completely reorganized. Zhu Guanzhi was appointed as the Chief of the First Section, Yao Quanxun as the Chief of the Second Section, Li Fangtong as the Director of the Cashier's Office, Zhou Chuanyu as the Director of Statistics, Zhu Manqing as the Director of Miscellaneous Taxes, and Tao Tiesheng as the Director of Land Taxes.

County Magistrate Concurrently Serves as Military Judge for Pacification The Jiangsu Pacification Commissioner has ordered that the Clear Township Bureaus in each county be gradually abolished. In the future, bandit cases will be handled according to judicial procedures, which are slow and time-consuming. Now that the green gauze tents are rising in the counties north of the Yangtze River and the bandits are stirring, and the counties along the lake south of the Yangtze River are clearing out lake bandits, the situation in each county and the strength of the bandits have been considered. The magistrates of 17 counties, including Nantong, Donghai, Ganyu

Page 10

, Yancheng, Pi County, Suining, Suqian, Guanyun, Shuyang, Liuhe, Funing, Rugao, Wujiang, Wujin, Yixing, Wu County, and Wuxi, have been selected and appointed to serve concurrently as military judges for pacification. Those who have been thoroughly investigated and tried in cases of theft, kidnapping, and red banditry may submit a request for approval to execute them in accordance with the Regulations on Punishing Thieves and Bandits, the Regulations on Punishing Kidnappers, and the Emergency Crime Punishment Law for Endangering the Republic of China.

General Headquarters Orders Knowledge of Borrowing the Poor People's Workshop The General Headquarters ordered the county government to be informed that the Army 11th Division's Injured Soldiers' Vocational Workshop, located in the Nantong Poor People's Workshop, is borrowed in nature and should not be misunderstood.

Return of Zhang Yu's Property Zhang Yu, a native of the county, was wanted by the former Military Affairs Commission in the autumn of 1927 for colluding with the enemy, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government was ordered to seal up his property. This year, Zhang Yu's son, Zhang Jing'an, requested the Ministry of Military Affairs to allow his father, who is old and senile, to be pardoned under the New Year's Day amnesty. "The approvals have been received, and the original case has been ordered to be revoked. A request has also been submitted to the Executive Yuan to order the Jiangsu Provincial Government to return the sealed property." The Executive Yuan, based on the report from the Ministry of Military Affairs, has issued an order to approve and has submitted the case to the National Government for the record, and has ordered the Jiangsu Provincial Government to investigate and handle the matter. All of Zhang Yu's property in Nantong and Dongtai will be returned in full upon the provincial order.

Temporary Court Temporarily Difficult to Establish The Nantong Temporary Court must await a decision from the Executive Yuan. More than 50 red bandits have been escorted back from Suzhou and are being held in the county government. Magistrate Zhang has submitted a request to the provincial government to separately imprison the criminals in the Fourth Prison and the court's detention center.

Establishment of a Tobacco Prohibition Investigation Office The Jiangsu Provincial Tobacco Prohibition Investigation Office has appointed Zhu Junfu as the Director of the Nantong Investigation Office. The office was established on the 30th in the new market in the south of the city. The office also has jurisdiction over the investigation affairs of Rugao, Haimen, and Qidong counties, each with a branch office. The chiefs of the branch offices have not yet been appointed.

Songjiang 61

Record of the Establishment of the Fengjing Township Chamber of Commerce: The preparations for the Fengjing Township Chamber of Commerce have been completed and approved by the relevant authorities. The inaugural meeting was held yesterday (the 1st). In the afternoon, the election of executive and supervisory committee members was held. As a result, Wu Difan, Wang Hanchen, Xu Beichen, Shi Yunyu, Yu Cuoyi, Wang Fangtao, Ge Maosheng, Jin Rumei, Pan Jinsheng, Ding Yufu, Fan Youshan, and others were elected as executive committee members. Lu Zaihong, Wang Langqiu, Hou Xikang, Xie Xiyan, and Xia Xinqian were elected as supervisory committee members. Subsequently, the first executive committee meeting was held, and standing committee members and a chairman were elected. Wu Difan, Wang Hanchen, and Wang Fangtao were elected as standing committee members, and Wu Difan was elected as chairman.

Special Commissioner for Prohibition of Opium Arrives in Songjiang: The Shanghai Investigation Office of the Opium Prohibition Committee has appointed Zhang Yuanpei as the special commissioner for opium prohibition in this county. He arrived in Songjiang yesterday to establish the office, renting the Zhang residence at Zhugan Hui as the office space. Letters were sent to the county government and the public security bureau for assistance. The internal organization includes investigation, general affairs, and other external affairs officers, including Wang Changqing, Yang Shijie, and Shen Jinrong, who are responsible for patrol and inspection duties. Currently, several townships have come forward to discuss undertaking the task.

Changzhou 62

Execution of Bandit Jin Yueliang: The Wuyi County Court previously received a bandit named Jin Yueliang who was apprehended. After interrogation, his crimes were confirmed, and he was sentenced to death. After submitting to higher authorities for approval and execution, the court's procuratorate dispatched police to bring the convict to the court at 8:00 AM on the second day, verified his identity, and escorted him to the Fengweidun execution ground for execution by firing squad.

Kidnapping Case Occurs in the Fifth District: He Yousheng, a resident of Xietouqiao Village near Hengshan Bridge in the Fifth District of Wuyi County, is a moderately wealthy man. His son is deceased, leaving behind a widow with a six-year-old child, living a lonely life. Unexpectedly, more than ten bandits, each armed with firearms, broke into the house and robbed them in the middle of the night on the 30th of last month. They also forced the widow to hand over her child. The bandits then took the child and fled north with a shout, warning her not to report the incident. The victim's family is currently negotiating the ransom.

Wuxi 63

Gu Wangqi Safely Escapes: Gu Wangqi, a villager from Gu Gengshang in Xicang Township of this county, was kidnapped from his home by bandits in the middle of the night on the 26th day of the old lunar calendar's fourth month, and his whereabouts were unknown. There were two false reports that he had been killed by the bandits, and corpses had been found, but none could be identified, so nothing could be confirmed. However, in the middle of the night the day before yesterday, Gu suddenly and safely escaped and returned home. According to his account, the kidnappers numbered six in total and spoke with Jiangyin and Changshu accents. They carried Browning pistols. After arriving at Gu's house, they first searched and looted a large bundle of clothes, then used cloth to blindfold Gu. They ran wildly to the northwest for about three miles before getting on a boat. The boat sailed all day, and only at night was the cloth removed. The boat was then moored in reeds surrounded by water. Subsequently, the bandit leader forced him to write a letter to his family to ask for money for his ransom, but Gu claimed that he couldn't write. The bandits were furious and said that no matter what, at least 1,000 yuan would be required to release him. He was held on the boat for more than ten days under strict guard. On the night before last, there was a thunderstorm, and Gu saw that the bandits guarding him were fast asleep. He then found a way to move the boat to the shore, went ashore, and escaped in secret. It took him two days and nights to escape back to his home.

Kidnapping and Robbery Cases Occur Continuously: Recently, robbery cases have been occurring continuously in the countryside. Just after the arrest of Qian Hai in the Tangtou Township robbery case, two more robbery cases occurred in Huangjiadang and Baojia Township. The details are as follows: (1) The Qian Xiexing Hotel in Huangjiadang at the intersection of the Xicheng Road in the Fifth District was broken into by bandits after 2:00 AM on the night before last, and two pieces of gold jewelry, worth a total of sixty or seventy yuan, were robbed. The victim reported the incident to the 13th Branch of the Public Security Bureau, which in turn reported it to the County Bureau for investigation. (2) In the Great King Temple in Baojiaqiao in the Second District, six bandits broke into the temple on the night of the 30th, pried open the door, dragged the temple caretaker Li Ada out of bed, and silenced him with threats. About two hundred yuan in clothes and silver was robbed. The district chief of the area has reported the case to the county and requested an investigation.

Sisters-in-law Disagree, Swallow Gold to Commit Suicide: Sun Qian, a young woman from Huangnitou outside the North Gate of this county, is 21 years old and works as a female worker in a silk factory in Dongmen. Her husband, surnamed Sun, works as a boatman. The couple's relationship is relatively harmonious, but she is unable to get along with her sisters-in-law and often argues with them. Sun Qian became depressed and unhappy, and before the Dragon Boat Festival, she rented a separate workshop to live in. However, her sisters-in-law did not allow her to live outside and urged her parents-in-law to persuade her to return. However, Qian felt that living with her sisters-in-law again would inevitably cause conflict, so she developed the idea of suicide. She swallowed a gold ring the day before yesterday, and the next day she swallowed another gold ring. The day after that, she swallowed a silver chain and a pair of gold bracelets. Finally, she secretly swallowed half a yuan of raw opium and lay down on the bed. In a moment, the poison took effect, her face turned pale, and her breathing became faint. Later, her husband noticed and immediately sent her to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. After the hospital's doctors made every effort to perform surgery, she was able to turn the corner and recover.

Yangzhou 64

Meeting of Singing Girls Scheduled: Gong Rongzhi, a supervisor of the County Public Security Bureau, was ordered to oversee the registration of singing girls. Each singing girl is required to pay 5 jiao as a fee for the Women's Relief Institute of the Relief Institute. Parents or representatives of singing girls were notified to attend a meeting on the 3rd at the Yangfang Study in Xin Street to discuss registration and regulations, which will be implemented immediately.

Traditional Chinese Medicine Doctor Wang Shaoquan Beaten: Xu Shizhong, who runs the Dadong Inn inside Dadongmen, hired Wang Shaoquan, a traditional Chinese medicine doctor from Beiliuxiang, to treat his sick son. The child died with blood flowing from both nostrils, and Xu believed that Wang's medicine had killed him. One day, he falsely claimed he wanted another consultation and brought Wang to the inn. As soon as he arrived, Xu closed the door and beat him severely. Wang's cries for help reached outside. Fortunately, a police officer on duty heard the cries and rushed to the rescue, breaking down the door and arresting both parties to be sent to the Second Precinct in charge, and then to the First Precinct for review and handling. The Chinese Medicine Association learned of this and immediately convened an emergency meeting of all Chinese medicine doctors in the afternoon to discuss how to respond.

Melon Farmers Rush to Repair the East Section of the Riverbank: The riverbank in Guazhou collapsed. Zang Liuge, the head of the Second Autonomous District in charge, supervised the people to rush to repair the western section, which was 270 zhang long. Because several dozen zhang of the eastern section between Majigang suddenly collapsed, in addition to planning to estimate the cost of 15,000 yuan for labor and materials and 5,000 yuan for digging soil and moving graves, he submitted a report to the county to be forwarded to the authorities, requesting that 15,000 yuan be raised locally, and the rest be allocated by the authorities. He also ordered district officers to beat gongs to gather three to four thousand people on the 29th to start emergency repairs in advance, using the Guanyin Temple as a temporary office, in order to prevent further collapse and protect the lives of the people.

Pinghu 65

A Mutiny Case from the Mouth of a Soldier: The truth about the mutiny and robbery and killing by the Provincial Security Team stationed in Xincang is still unknown. Two of the fleeing soldiers have now been apprehended in Zhangyan Town, Jiangsu Province, and sent to the Second Regiment of the Jiangsu Security for interrogation. According to Zhang Shiyong, 19 years old, from Ningbo, who joined the 9th Squad of the company as a second-class soldier in April of this year, and Fang Fengtian, from Jiangxi, 22 years old, who joined the 9th Squad of the company as a first-class soldier last year, the incident occurred because the 16th Company's First Platoon was stationed in Xincang, the Second Platoon was stationed in Xinmiao, and the Third Platoon was stationed in Yaqian. The squad leader, Hu Bin, secretly used civilian telephones to communicate information. At 12:00 on the night of June 22, Hu Bin seized the wooden-cased gun of the Third Platoon leader and tied him up with a rope. He then ordered the brothers of each squad to load their bullets, led them to Xincang, and arrived at 1:30 AM. They met with the First and Second Platoons, all of whom were under the command of the Second Platoon Leader Zhou. Zhou sent the First Platoon to monitor the Public Security Bureau, and the Second and Third Platoons to stand guard. The Fourth Platoon leader led his subordinates to the Fourth District Office to borrow military pay. District Chief Zhu refused, so Hu Bin fired a shot and injured his foot, and they obtained 300 yuan. The robbery began at 4:30 AM. It was still dark, and the pawnshops were not open. Fearing that the army would come to suppress them, they did not dare to stay long. After about half an hour, they formed a line, led by a local guide, and rushed to Zhapu, arriving at 8:00 AM in the morning. They robbed a pawnshop for about an hour, then crossed the sea by boat. The boat I was on had 34 people. The remaining two boats were behind. When they arrived in Haiyan, they were pursued and disarmed by the security force. At 3:00 PM, they arrived at the Putuo Temple in the Outer Sea Mountains and stayed for one day. At 9:00 PM on the 24th, the 34 people went to Baisha Bay together and encountered the security force again. Because it was already dark, they were able to escape. That night, they fled to Jinshan. They were just thinking of taking a ship to Shanghai when they were apprehended in Zhangyan. The silver robbed this time was all in the possession of Platoon Leader Zhou and the squad leaders. We only received five yuan in military pay, etc. The two soldiers are still detained in the Second Regiment of the Jiangsu Security and will probably be sent here within a few days.

Demolition Begins on the Ancient Hall of the North Temple: The Great Hero Hall of the North Temple, commonly known as the Imperial Hall, was built during the Huichang era of the Tang Dynasty, more than 1,000 years ago, and is the oldest building in this county. However, due to years of disrepair, the eaves on the north side have collapsed beyond repair. Neither the public nor private sectors have funds to repair it. The local government has now hired workers to demolish it. It is said that the Buddhist Association also supports this move. Work began on the 29th.

Jiaxing 66

Completion of Parasitic Wasp Protection Room: Biological control is a new trend in modern pest control. Therefore, the Zhejiang Provincial Plant Disease and Pest Control Institute has designated using insects to control insects as one of the control policies. However, the results of the large-scale purchase of rice borer egg masses in Jiangzhe over the years have often been burned, resulting in the destruction of both good and bad. The parasitic wasps, which are most effective in killing rice borer eggs, are also destroyed, which defeats the purpose of pest control. Wu Fuzhen, director of the Zhejiang Provincial Plant Disease and Pest Control Institute, recognizing this, after careful planning, cooperated with the Jiaxing County Pest Control Association to build a large-scale parasitic wasp protection and experimental room in Jiaxing. It has been exactly one month since construction began, and it has now been completed. The opening ceremony was held at 2:00 PM on June 28. Director Wu personally attended, and the Jiaxing County Administrative Commissioner and members of the Pest Control Committee also attended the ceremony.

Huzhou 67

Police and Bandits Exchange Fire, Intercept Bandit Boat: Jiang Boxiong, the chief of the Third District of the Nanxun Water Police, received a report from civilians the day before yesterday that four bandit boats with about 30 bandits had been discovered in the Hengguqiao area outside the west shed of Nanxun. After receiving the report, the district chief ordered Guo, the leader of the 5th Platoon of the 10th Squad, to lead more than 30 water police officers to suppress and capture the bandits. When the squad arrived at Jiuliqiao, they saw the bandit boats heading east. The two sides immediately exchanged fire for about two hours. The bandits were unable to resist and fled ashore. Two bandit boats were captured, and two bandits, Duan Dejin and Duan Yongyou, were captured, and one hostage was rescued. The squad took them back for interrogation. It has been heard that the hostage is Zhu Xingsheng from Nihe Dou in Shuanglin, who was kidnapped by bandits last month. District Chief Jiang has now notified the family to come and claim him.

Bandits Intercept Civilian Boat: A resident of Hongxingqiao in Huzhou hired Xie Zirong, a relative, to come to Huzhou by boat yesterday to pick up his two sons who were studying at a school in this city, as the summer vacation has arrived. Unexpectedly, when passing the ferry crossing of Yangjiazhuang, about seven li from this city, two bandits, each holding a pistol, shouted for them to stop the boat. The boatman, seeing that the bandits had weapons, had to dock the boat and let the bandits get on board and search. All the cash that Xie had with him was robbed.

Letter

Letter from Lawyer Jin Yu 68

To Whom It May Concern,

I have recently received a statement from my client, Ms. Yang Shuzhen, claiming that in the "Suzhou Communication" news item published in the Outer Ports Communication column on the third page of the Shen Bao on June 4 of this year, the headline was "Hu Zhiqin Divorce Case Appealed and Settled," and the content stated that Hu Zhiqin served as a clerk in a cloth store at the age of sixteen and fell in love with Yang Shuzhen, a woman from Changzhou who lived next door to the store. Later, they rented a place to live in in Jiumudi. Hu suspected that Yang was having an affair with his friend Wang Jingfei, which led to quarrels and a breakup, and a divorce agreement was signed. Later, Hu suddenly asked Yang Shuzhen for subsidies for losses, etc. These details are not entirely accurate. The marriage agreement in this case was arranged by a matchmaker at Hu Zhiqin's request and was not a casual affair. The reason for the termination of the agreement was that Hu Zhiqin was addicted to smoking and unemployed, and had fallen in love with someone else. The statement in the news that Hu rented a house for them to live together is not true. The original report disclosing the above news occurred when she was bedridden and unable to move. Now, after a friend informed her of the situation, she feels that her reputation is at stake. Such distortion of facts is likely to cause confusion. Therefore, she has entrusted this lawyer to send a letter on her behalf, requesting a correction. I am writing this letter to request your newspaper to investigate and make the correction. Sincerely,

Lawyer Jin Yu

June 29

Russian, Legal, and Art Colleges Oppose Change to Specialized Status

Shanghai Municipal Elementary School Joint Graduation Ceremony 73

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau held the fourth joint graduation ceremony for elementary schools yesterday. More than 3,000 graduates, faculty, staff, and guests from various schools attended, making it a grand occasion. Zheng, Section Chief of the Municipal Education Bureau, presided over the meeting on behalf of the Director, and Zhang Angqian served as the recorder. The general situation is described below:

Chairman's Report: Briefly stated that the city has a population of more than 3 million, but the city's schools and registered private elementary schools have only 2,759 graduates this time, including 1,518 graduates from city schools and 1,841 graduates from private schools. He hopes that the number of graduates from various schools will gradually increase in the future in order to achieve the goal of universal education in the city. Today's elementary school graduation ceremony held by this bureau has three meanings. The first is to make all the children understand that they have now completed national education. Elementary education is also called national education. Those who have completed national education are healthy citizens. Healthy citizens are people who are healthy in knowledge, morality, and physical fitness. They are adults, not children. After today's graduation ceremony, you, children, will be responsible, independent, and self-governing members of society, no longer dependent on parents and teachers like before. This is the first meaning of holding this ceremony, to call everyone's attention. The second is to make everyone understand that you have now completed basic education. Elementary education can also be called basic education. Elementary education is the foundation of all education, and it will be easy to gradually improve in the future. Children, you have learned the Party Ideology, Chinese, Arithmetic, Social Studies, Nature, and other courses of elementary school, and you have a foundation for all courses. You can already write, speak, read, calculate, and know about the major events of the Party and the country, the major events of the world, and the phenomena of the natural world. From now on, whether you go to work or go to school, if you want to study on your own or go to a higher-level school to study, it will be like a daily progress because you have a foundation, and you can definitely expect to be successful. This is the second point of today's ceremony to call everyone's attention. The third is to make everyone understand that you have now completed elementary education. Elementary education can also be called elementary education. Studying must follow the order and cannot be skipped. The ancients said that those who travel far must start from the near, and those who climb high must start from the low. Today, you have completed the first stage of elementary education, and you have already started to walk through the door of knowledge. From middle school to university, the future is unlimited. The beginning still cannot but start from elementary education. This is the third kind of meaning of today's ceremony to call everyone's attention. In short, the education business is no different from planting flowers. When you first entered elementary school, it was like a flower had sprouted. Every day, the educational administrative organs and the teachers of various schools worked hard to irrigate it, helping it to grow. Today, you have graduated from elementary school, just like a flower has buds. After that, you will go to school or build a career in society, and in the future, you will bloom and bear fruit. The future is bright. I urge all children to work hard.

Speech by the Mayor's Representative: Briefly stated that your graduation today is like a flower gradually blooming and bearing fruit. It is expected that the future will be realized and shine brightly, otherwise it will be a dark and dangerous future. At this time of great progress, the children who graduate in the future should cherish their precious youth, eliminate difficulties, and overcome the environment.

Chen Heqin's Speech: Briefly stated that today is one of the most glorious days for you children. It is hoped that you will be beautiful flowers and gradually full. Whether you go to school or work, you should pay attention to the word "learn." Edison's invention of science and the Prime Minister's not forgetting to read during the revolutionary period are all excellent models. As for the two words "be a person," you must also pay attention to how to imitate the Prime Minister's revolutionary spirit and studious spirit in order to contribute to society in the future. Subsequently, Li Bojun, the representative of the city school principal, and Li Yunbing, the representative of the school principal, gave speeches. Finally, the representatives of Wanzhu School, the graduate of the city school, and the representatives of Zijin School, the graduates of the private school, answered, and the meeting adjourned.

Labor University Students Request Continued Enrollment of New Students 74

The National Labor University University Department's Declaration on the Ministry of Education's Second Suspension of Enrollment states: The laborers of the world have gradually awakened since the European Revolution, and are eager to break away from their historical shackles. Therefore, the labor movement has also occurred in China. With the development of the Three Principles of the People and the National Revolution, Chinese laborers are even more eager to obtain thorough liberation from now on. The purpose of this university is to comply with this trend of the times and to experiment with labor education and cultivate leadership talents to implement labor education. This is a well-known fact. Among the people of China, the toiling farmers and workers constitute the absolute majority. In order to complete the Chinese revolution, we must base it on the masses of farmers and workers. This is the reason why Prime Minister Sun Yat-sen first made the policy for farmers and workers, the meaning of which is to train the masses of farmers and workers to participate in the revolution, and improve their skills, strengthen their organizations, transform their lives, and enable them to obtain true liberation and complete the highest task of the revolution. This university was officially announced to be established in the autumn of the 16th year for this purpose. Since its establishment, this university has always attached equal importance to academic theory and technology and has cultivated the spirit of laborers in order to prepare to go deep into the ranks of the masses of farmers and workers. Its education system and meaning are completely different from ordinary universities. Compared with the Central Political School and the Military Academy, which train practical military and political talents, it is exactly the same. This is the special significance of the existence of this university. Although it has only been four years since its establishment, we dare not boast about how perfect the content is, and the speed of development is comparable to history. However, it can also be said to be quite gratifying. In principle, as this university, the product of the revolution, is in the process of development, the Ministry of Education, which bears the highest educational administrative responsibility of the country, should fulfill its responsibility to love and supervise it. Unexpectedly, in the autumn of last year, it was suspended from enrolling new students under the pretext of mismanagement and for the sake of rectification, causing poor children to look forward to hope in vain, and complaints can be seen on the front pages of newspapers. Its only hope is to be able to enroll new students again this year. Therefore, on the day after the enrollment advertisement was published in the newspaper, more than 800 letters requesting enrollment brochures were received. From this, it can be seen that the number of poor children who are out of school is large, and the desire to go to school is strong. Unfortunately, the enrollment advertisement was only published for two days before it was ordered to stop enrollment again in the name of rectification. It seems that this is not the original intention of the Ministry of Education to love labor education, and it is deeply alarming to all the students of this university. (To be continued)

World Heavyweight Boxing Match Tonight at 10 p.m. 82

Former champion Schmeling vs. Stribling

German Max Schmeling won the World Heavyweight Boxing Championship because American Jack Sharkey violated the rules. Time flies, and it has already been a year. Tonight at 10 p.m., German Schmeling will re-enter the boxing ring to make his first attempt to defend his controversial championship title, striving to deal with the Kiowa William Stribling. The two heroes will meet at the Cleveland Municipal Stadium in Ohio, USA, for a fifteen-round battle to compete for this year's championship.

New York Committee Changes Attitude 83

Withdraws recognition; New York has no championship

Max Schmeling's victory and Jack Sharkey's violation of the rules were based on the opinion of the New York Athletic Commission. Later, Schmeling refused Sharkey's request for a rematch, so the New York Committee felt dissatisfied and resolutely withdrew Schmeling's championship. New York therefore has no official championship for this event. However, public opinion, as well as the world sports community and the American National Boxing Association, remain consistent in their recognition.

Schmeling's Skills Declining After Success 84

Returns home in glory to enjoy happiness

Schmeling has fought five major battles in the past two years, four in 1929, consecutively defeating Josie Gara, Pietro Gori, Joe Nameth, and Paulino Uzcudun. After his final battle, his victory over Jack Sharkey, he held the championship, returned home in glory, and lived a peaceful and happy life. Within a year, he disappeared from the boxing ring, and his skills inevitably declined. Starting this year, he went on a performance tour of the United States to reorganize his forces.

Stribling Rises Up 85

Highly acclaimed as a fierce general on the battlefield

Stribling is 27 years old, one year older than Schmeling, and they weigh the same, about 195 pounds each. In the past year, he defeated Phil Scott, frustrated Dave Griffith, and defeated Ansett Dicko, creating a fervent clamor. He has had 260 matches in his career, long known as a fierce general on the battlefield. He is the only good player in Kiowa, having defeated local hero Palip Makanira, so most people expect Stribling to have a good chance of winning within fifteen rounds. Given that Jack Sharkey almost overwhelmed Schmeling before his foul, Stribling may reenact this scene.

The Competition Venue is Great and Amazing 86

Can accommodate as many as 110,000 people

This competition will shake the world and is sure to be a success. The Cleveland Municipal Stadium is great and amazing, capable of accommodating 110,000 people. The future ticket revenue will be about $1.5 million. The total management on stage is by Dr. 　 Lipton. This was originally in New York's Madison Square Garden, but because the New York Committee withdrew its recognition of Schmeling's championship, it was moved here, so this great competition was able to avoid the risk of interruption.

Free Talk

A Word of Gain 98

— Yi Mei

Religious people say, the soul is immortal. Scientists say, matter is indestructible. And ordinary young men and women say, love is indestructible.

Three parts of wine are for prosperity, seven parts of wine are for moral decay.

Why did the ancients have to create the word "old," causing countless sages, heroes, beautiful women, and talented men in later generations to be ruined in this word "old." The vast sea, Jingwei can hardly fill, I hate it.

Navigating the sea of learning, there is no worry of sinking ships.

What the world values is not necessarily pleasing to my heart. What the world hates is not necessarily hateful to my eyes.

Sweeping away the watermelon peels and fruit shells on the ground, it is a great pleasure.

Fighting for internal strife, death is as light as a feather. Fighting for external regret, death is heavier than Mount Tai.

Chickens are hygienists, getting up early is creation. Crickets are elegant scholars, singing and enjoying themselves.

A magistrate is ashamed of receiving a salary when the people are fleeing. I wonder how many of today's public officials have such thoughts.

Mountains are far and passes are blocked, only dreams can pass. The earth is long and the sky is long, this love is endless.

The curtain ripples slightly, and the ice mat is sweet in dreams. I am ashamed as a hard worker, unable to experience it.

Women loving talent is just a plot in novels. It is rarely seen in reality.

People love the colorful world, I sigh at the fleeting life.

Talks of a Guest Returning from Western Hubei 99

— Old Farmer of Tian Yu

Mr. Hu Hezhang, my old friend. Last year he went to Western Hubei for business, and it has been a year now. He came to Shanghai yesterday and stayed at the Central Hostel. After hearing the news, I drove to visit him and asked about the situation there. Mr. Hu said that since the Red bandits sneaked into Xingshan, it is not far from Yichang. So the market is still peaceful. However, there is a female flying guard among the Red bandits, who is fierce and poisonous. It can be described.

The Origin of the Female Flying Guard: The female flying guard is He Ying, the younger sister of He Long, the leader of the Red bandits. She is only over twenty years old, slender, with a delicate face, and has infinite strength. She is skilled in shooting. Holding a gun, she rushes into battle, and every bullet hits the target. The bandits are amazed by her supernatural skills and are all in awe. Because of her beauty and marksmanship, the bandits call her the female flying guard. Flying Guard has an inherently sinister, fierce, and cruel nature, even more than He Long. She also trained a female army of a thousand people, equipped with guns, to assist her brother and trample on various places. The victims are countless.

The Strange Clothing of the Female Army: The female army trained by Flying Guard are all village women from various places in Hubei and Hunan who have been incited to follow. They are all under thirty years old, physically strong, and die in battle. No less than men. And their clothing is the most strange. The clothes are tight and narrow, the shorts reach the knees, bare feet with straw sandals, and red cloth is wrapped around the calves for easy walking. The clothes are black for easy hiding. A slit is cracked in the middle of the shorts for urination. The hair is combed on top of the head, like a wandering Taoist priest from Maoshan. The strange shapes are difficult to describe.

Releasing Sky Lanterns, Dissecting Abdomen and Gutting Intestines: The Red bandits must torture the rich among the villagers in various ways to force out their hidden gold. After that, they strip off their clothes and trousers, tie them naked to a tree, and soak their whole bodies with cotton wool soaked in kerosene, then set them on fire, calling it releasing sky lanterns. Or they use sharp knives to dissect their abdomen and gut their intestines, which is inhumane.

The National Army Encirclement and Suppression Sneaked into Xingshan: The Red bandits originally based in Shihe, Cili, and Feng Counties in Hubei, with strong strength. Since Mr. Xu Yuanquan served as the Qingxiang Superviser of the three provinces of Sichuan, Hubei, and Hunan, they have attacked many times. He Long has repeatedly lost battles, and his strength has been greatly damaged. The official army's morale is high. The female flying guard discussed with her brother that in order to preserve her strength, she had to abandon the area and led the remnants of seven or eight thousand bandits overnight, crossing Badong Zigui, and sneaking into Xingshan. Because the mountains there are steep, they can resist. It is now heard that Mr. Xu will order an attack within days in order to thoroughly eliminate the bandit forces.

Guiding Tour of Mount Lu 100

— Shen Tingkai

Looking horizontally, it is a ridge, looking sideways, it is a peak. Distant and near, high and low, each is different. Not knowing the true face of Mount Lu, it is only because you are in the midst of this mountain. I read this poem by Su Dongpo, the poet master of the Song Dynasty. Recalling a tour of Mount Lu in the summer of the eighteenth year, carefully tasting the taste, I can't help but long for the time of two years. Like the flowing water in the Yangtze River, it flows slowly. I don't know how much memory of other things has drifted away. But the thousands of cliffs and valleys of Mount Lu, and the sound of springs everywhere, can never drift away. Let me record my tour and use it as a record of a past event, or as a guide for the journey of gentlemen and ladies.

To go to Mount Lu from Shanghai, you can take a plane or a boat. First go to Jiujiang from Shanghai, and then transfer to the destination. But although the plane is fast, most people dare not try it. It takes three whole days to reach by boat. So those who are experienced in travel have come up with an expedient itinerary, which is to take the Beijing-Shanghai night express train to Beijing, and then take a boat to the destination from Xiaguan the next morning. In about forty hours, you can reach Jiujiang.

The center of Mount Lu is, of course, Guling. When you arrive in Jiujiang, change to a car (about 1.7-8 yuan per person). Amidst the constant sound of clear springs, you arrive at Lotus Cave on the mountainside. After getting off the car, walk or go up by shoulder chair. I took a shoulder chair. Step by step up the mountain. At first, it was very hot. Later, the higher you go, the cooler it becomes. Gradually, you don't feel the heat anymore. Looking at the Western-style houses of Guling, a corner of the red building is revealed from the depths of the green shade. Looking down at the scenery of the Yangtze River, it is really majestic and beautiful.

Guling is high above sea level. The scenery of the Yangtze River is really majestic and beautiful. It was originally a leased area operated by the British pastor Littell, so the equipment is extremely comprehensive. There are schools, hotels, hospitals, clubs, sports fields, swimming pools, etc. After our country took back the leased area, it did not diminish in color.

If you search all the scenic spots in the entire Mount Lu, it is really impossible to search them all. So you can only use Guling as a base for exploring nearby. But although I traveled happily for more than ten days, the places I missed were countless.

The impression that I will never forget is the moonlit night tour of Bailu Cave. That day, I first went to Hanpokou to see the clouds. Suddenly the peak was covered and disappeared. Suddenly it opened up again, and the weather was unpredictable. After watching the clouds, I immediately went down the mountain. When I arrived at the foot of the mountain, I followed the huge spring and passed Qixian Temple (Cihang Temple) to Bailu Cave. What touched my eyes was a wooden archway with the words "Happy Land of Famous Teachings." Passing Liufang Bridge and entering the gate of Bailu Academy, I suddenly heard the sound of reading aloud, and I felt that the legacy of Huiweng in the past is still there today. There is a couplet next to the courtyard that says, "Deer and pigs play together, a place to forget things. Springs and peaks reflect each other, wisdom and benevolence are uniquely obtained." After returning from Bailu Cave, I went back to Cihang Temple to spend the night. The feeling this night is much happier than a newly married couple. Late at night, a gust of clear wind made a sound, and the temple bell kept ringing. I turned to think about the floating clouds and human affairs, and I couldn't help but want to be a long-time companion with the ancient Buddha and Qingdeng.

The temples and Taoist temples in Mount Lu include Tianchi Temple, Donglin Temple, Xilin Temple, Zhanyun Temple, Qixian Temple, Xiufeng Temple, and Cihang Temple. The famous mountain peaks include Wulao Peak, Xianglu Peak, Shuangjian Peak, Lianhua Peak, Plow Peak, and Hanyang Peak. Famous places include Buddha Hand Rock, Yubei Pavilion, Bailu Cave, Huanglongtan, and Sanxia Ravine.

The Pine Forest is a scenic spot in Guling. It stretches for a very long time and is especially quiet. We walk among them, feeling that the mountains are green, the pines are also green, and people in the jungle seem to be reflected in green clothes and green faces. Especially the couples, walking in pairs under the forest, making people think that they only envy mandarin ducks and not immortals.

Finally, I hope that the gentlemen and ladies who travel to Mount Lu will also find it valuable to stay in Xunyang when they go out of Xunyang. Looking at Mount Lu from the shores of Gantang Lake in Xunyang, the true face cannot be distinguished. This scene and this feeling are also thought-provoking.

Butterfly Loves Flowers 101

— Bin Hong

Wandering thoughts are like willow catkins. Turning around a hundred times, it is already a mistake in this life. Peeking at people under the curtain, caught by the wind. Where will the thousands of tendernesses go? Illness and poetry become obstacles. Small pavilion and sparse lattice, loving the moon deeply. Suddenly recalling that the waves can understand language, the hair is low and surrounded by countless mountains.

Inscription for the Play "Liu Rushi" by the Master of Small Liu Fragrance 102

— Song Tuo

Who can compare with Jing in the elegance of the old generation? It is pitiful to die a difficult death. Tender feelings are more important than group grace. Willing to fail the Qing even if it is changed to Jiangshan.

The shadows of Qinhuai are still in the world. Broadcast into new voices and win smiles. The joys and sorrows of Sangyu are different. Fanshan is ultimately better than Yushan.

Travelogue to India (60) 103

— Ling Hua

Now this kind of movement is all started by Indians. If the Chinese people can advance with it, then the matter of Asian liaison is very easy. Even Japan has no difficulty in urging it to wake up, slightly slowing down its ambition to be small and easy to fill, and jointly seeking the progress of Asian civilization. The people of the three islands do not worry about not having food to eat. This point is especially worth noting. If the Chinese can unite with the Indians to unite Japan in the east and the Hui in the west in order to restore the true civilization of Asia, abandon narrow nationalism, and realize Sun Yat-sen's Datongism, it may not be impossible to implement it in Asia first. Although Japan does not seem to be a big obstacle, it is also in the movement. As for the British Confucian Wells, he once advocated that China and the United States should unite first, and then merge with Europe, because Europe is prone to chaos and there is no hope for peace. Therefore, it is hoped that China and the United States in the Pacific Ocean will be the pioneers of world Datong. It can also be seen that Eastern culture has a tendency to become the center of the 20th century. Truth will win the final victory. China should encourage itself.

Two children, only thirteen or four years old, do not understand English very well. They came to my room. Eagerly asking for their intention, they are willing to follow me to China. I asked that their parents and brothers are all in India, why do they want to go to China. They answered that I am very willing to travel to China. I love China too. I took out a statue of Guanyin and showed it to them, saying, this is the goddess of China and Japan. Every household enshrines it. You should know that this Bodhisattva is very powerful. They do not understand very much. I said, you look closely and know that the appearance of this goddess is no different from the decoration of your mother and sisters. They agreed. I said, this can know the relationship between Indian and East Asian culture. More than a thousand years ago, I translated your classics and imitated your goddess, occupying the entire power in East Asia. It is still popular today. Your India is like a big tree, and the flowers are all over Asia. In the future, you will be welcomed when you come to the East. But you are still young now, and you cannot even speak English. It can be when you grow up. They left with mixed feelings of grief and joy. Do not neglect this small matter. It can prove that young children have such admiration for China, which is the best phenomenon. This is because their philosophers heard that Chinese celebrities had arrived and wanted to cry. Young children heard that China was traveling like this, and they could predict the future relationship.

A student named Sami Nanda lives in Conak County, very close to Kushinagar. Kushinagar is the place where the Buddha entered Nirvana, that is, the place where the Nirvana Sutra was said. He is willing to guide me to his home to see the place where the Buddha entered Nirvana. It is not far from Varanasi, and it is said that there is a great hope that Chinese Buddhism schools will be established there. If they can be established, many small kings in India are also happy to donate money, because the Westerners who run Christianity also donate money. Buddha is the Buddha of India. Indians are naturally happy to support Buddhism. However, Indians themselves have not yet been able to promote it. They hope that the Chinese will promote it and the Indians will help it. According to me, the small European country of Sweden has even sent people to Shanxi in northern China to collect snake species. I used to live with them. They collected various snakes and returned to the small countries of Sweden and Denmark, and the missionaries spread all over the earth. It is because they are promoting their civilization as the crown. Now that China is so big, I do not know what work the millions of Buddhists are doing, and they do not even repay the kindness of the Indian Buddhist land. Is it not pitiful? May the Buddhists encourage themselves.

Novel Club Round Table

Unspecified Title（10） 104

— Xu Zhuodai

After a while, there was no sound on the floor above, and Ziliang thought she was done dancing. After being disturbed by her, now that she was finished, I could get to work. But before long, the sound rose again:

"Drizzling rain, falling non-stop..."

She raised her loud throat and began to sing loudly. How could Ziliang concentrate on his work? He had no choice but to put down his pen and wait for the storm to subside.

"I don't want your gold, I don't want your silver, I only want your heart, ah ya ya! Your heart..."

Ziliang's heart was truly being taken away by her. He couldn't bear it any longer and walked to the top of the stairs:

"What's all the racket? Singing this kind of song, how old are you this year?"

"This old woman is seventy-two years old, haha!"

"Acting like a little kid, why don't you go downstairs!"

Having said that, he returned to his small room. The madam had indeed left. As she was going down the stairs, she stuck her head into the small room:

"Schoolteachers don't deserve to appreciate art,"

A burst of wild laughter and footsteps went down the stairs together. He heard her go to the kitchen, probably to prepare the dishes. Ziliang regrouped and picked up his pen again to correct his students' compositions.

After reading about half of one, the madam's mumbling could be heard on the stairs:

"Women depend on men for their livelihood, so I, Yueru, can't be without my husband Pan Ziliang for a moment!"

As soon as she finished speaking, she had already stepped into the small room. Ziliang saw that she was holding a steelyard in her right hand, with a wine cup in the balance pan. A look of embarrassment appeared on her face:

"Can you help me calculate! According to my cookbook, I should use two liang of soy sauce; but this is a newly made steelyard, and the weight is different from before. I'm afraid it will be too much!"

"Nonsense!"

"If the amount of soy sauce is not calculated according to the cookbook, and the dish doesn't taste good, I can't be responsible."

Ziliang knew that if he didn't calculate it for her, firstly, she wouldn't go downstairs, and secondly, today's dish would be ruined. So, he used his pen to calculate on the paper:

"Use one liang, six qian, eight fen, seven li and a half!"

Ziliang deliberately did not round the decimals, otherwise she might ask questions repeatedly. At this moment, as soon as she heard "one liang, six qian, eight fen, seven li and a half," without even asking how to weigh it, she frowned, holding the steelyard in her right hand and a cup of soy sauce in her left, and went downstairs.

The Seventh Shanghai Municipal Representative Conference Continued Yesterday 105

Over Fifty Important Cases Were Resolved on the Spot

The Conference Adjourned at 5 PM on the Same Day

The Seventh Representative Conference of the Kuomintang Shanghai Special Municipality opened on July . Forty-two candidates for executive and supervisory committee members were elected that day, as detailed in yesterday's newspaper. The conference continued at 9 AM yesterday, with 58 representatives in attendance, chaired by Wang Yansong, with Chen Boxiu and Li Jiran as recorders. The meeting adjourned at 12 PM. It reconvened at 1 PM, chaired by Wu Kaixian, with 52 representatives in attendance. Over fifty proposals were resolved on the spot. The proceedings are summarized as follows:

Report of the Review Committee: Following the chairman's lead in observing the formalities, Cai Hongtian of the Proposal Review Committee reported on the review of the proposals. A total of 59 proposals were received, of which 35 were approved, 8 were rejected, 9 were deemed unnecessary for discussion at the conference and were referred to the next report committee, and 7 were consolidated for discussion, totaling 59 proposals.

Should it be appropriate, we respectfully await your public decision. Resolution: Consolidated with Case 6.
